Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Two Terrifying Knives 232

— Yang An

Due to the impact of the global economic recession, all countries are unanimously taking promoting their goods as the only way out. In addition to promoting goods, they are also building high tariff barriers to prevent the inflow of foreign goods. As a result, Country A defends against Country B, and Country B defends against Country C. To put it bluntly, they only want their goods to flow into other countries, and do not allow other countries' goods to be imported domestically. Look at the recent days, the Anglo-Japanese conference, the Anglo-French conference, as well as the British Parliament's urgency and the American people's panic, are all due to this problem. Among them, you tighten me, you are fierce, I am strong. The most pitiful is none other than our China, and the most deserving of death is none other than our national products industry. We do not have the right to set our own tariffs, and there is no way to ban foreigners from setting up factories. As a result, there is a trade deficit of 700 million yuan, and in the recent one or two months, the monthly trade deficit has been more than 100 million yuan. The dumping of Japanese goods is like mercury seeping into the ground, leaving no gap untouched. The tide-like influx of Japanese goods is just beginning. Not satisfied with dumping, they have recently taken action to set up factories extensively in China. One knife chokes the head, and another knife holds the wrist, and my dying national products industry has no possibility of resistance. This situation is not only pitiful, but also painful and sad. Those who run national product businesses suffer so much, but those in power have no intention of sympathizing, and impose heavy taxes, draining the pond to catch all the fish. The labor unrest that rises and falls from east to west is unfortunately triggered everywhere, strangling the industrial world to death. A certain gentleman said very sadly: "Running a national product factory is not something humans can do." What distressed words these are. Therefore, I do not hope for anything else, but hope that the government will quickly see the dangerous state of the factories and rescue them from their urgent plight. Workers should realize the difficulties of the factories and work together to support their progress, so that everyone can survive. All Chinese citizens should use their conscience to buy national products to save themselves and save the country.

National Products Year and Trade Deficit By Bao Cunming 233

—

All animals with blood have a strong resistance to external oppression. Even if they cannot use active methods to launch a head-on attack, at least——especially humans, I think——because they are all spiritual and understanding——they will also use a passive method, swearing to boycott to show that their spirit has not been subjected to any surrender.

In the current situation in China, with material construction being so immature and military defense being so lax, the only way to resist stubborn enemies is of course passive. The fact is so, and I do not find it hateful that the government is unwilling to send troops on a large scale, but I cannot help but have some doubts about the responsibilities within the reach of every citizen's power.

According to the most reliable survey, China's trade situation last year was:

Total Imports 728,333,916 yuan

Total Exports 315,485,016 yuan

Trade Deficit 412,848,900 yuan

This is truly a very strange phenomenon. In the past, when we did not advocate national products, mark a National Products Year, and resist foreign economic aggression——although there were several partial promotions of national products and eight or nine boycotts of Japanese and foreign goods, but none were as serious as this time——although there were also trade deficits, the amount was not so large. Moreover, this time it is still the "National Products Year" after everyone suffered great humiliation and shouted themselves hoarse!

Compatriots! The existence or demise of a country depends on the spirit of its people. War is secondary. Advocating national products and resisting foreign economic oppression is the expression of national spirit. If the trade deficit continues to increase annually as it is now, then the Chinese national spirit is dead. In other words, China has the possibility of immediate demise.

This is not intentionally saying unlucky things. The fact is indeed so. The reason why the amount of the trade deficit is so huge is all created by every citizen. According to the total imports last year, on average, everyone bought two yuan of foreign goods in the National Products Year. Do you think it is strange or not? In short, everything must start from reality. Merely shouting "National Products Year," "Women's National Products Year," "×× National Products Year" is not effective.

What I Should Do for Women's National Products Year 234

— Shan

Using national products is everyone's inherent duty; it cannot be accomplished solely by a portion of young people or women. It requires the joint promotion of all our beloved compatriots. If we can use them with one heart and one mind, I think we will definitely be able to completely eliminate imported goods.

Women also bear a great responsibility for promoting national products; however, this year is Women's National Products Year, so the responsibility they bear is even more significant. I will now put aside all empty talk and only talk about the work I should do for this year's Women's National Products Year, as briefly described below!

(1) In terms of clothing, food, and housing——I am determined not to use foreign goods for my needs in clothing, food, and housing, but only use national products; if any of the three items are unavailable in national products, I will resolutely replace them with other items. If my compatriots use one less cent of foreign goods, they will recover one cent of rights for the country. I hope the sisters in my circle will work hard to do this.

(2) Persuade my husband——If my husband likes to use foreign goods, I should earnestly persuade him to stop using them. If he repeatedly refuses to listen to my persuasion, I will resolutely use the words "divorce" to prompt him to realize his mistake.

(3) Things used by children——If I already have children, then I will never buy foreign toys or other items for my children, but will buy national products across the board.

(4) Persuade relatives and friends to use national products——For relatives and friends who like to use foreign goods, I should persuade them with very sincere words, so that they understand that the reason why our country's national products cannot be promoted is because all compatriots are unwilling to use national products, so all the merchants have no choice but to smuggle foreign goods. Dear relatives and friends! You must understand that the more money we give them, the more bullets they will make. Looking at it this way, isn't it dangerous? Relatives and friends! Can you really not use national products?

The four points mentioned above are all clichés. I am afraid that you are unwilling to read them again, right? However, I always hope that all the young people and sisters can implement them in this way. I think this year's Women's National Products Year will definitely achieve great results.

The Position of Women in the National Products World By Zhang Mengzhao 235

—

There is an old saying: "Those who respect others are always respected by others, and those who love others are always loved by others." That is to say: If you respect and love others, others will also respect and love you. I want to put it another way: If you respect and love the country and love national products, others will also respect your personality! Women—under the feudal legacy, have always been looked down upon in society! Now everyone is raising the status of women, and the situation is different. This year is designated as "Women's National Products Year" because if the women's world can love and use national products, then women have the ability to turn things around! In the text "Feminine Views of Ancient and Modern Philosophers" translated by Mr. Lang Lixun: His prelude is "In the past, although women's position in society was dominated by male power, all social activities were actually centered on women. Husbands in the family all obeyed their wives. The family is a cell of the social organization, so all social activities, although attributed to men, they are puppets, and those who pull the strings behind the scenes are actually women. Men's activities are just gestures." I am very confident that Mr. Lang's words are absolutely right!

(1) Mrs. Karan Mirquet Alice said: A woman's smile! Is a universal language.

(2) Filon said: Men will not achieve anything without the help of women in action!

(3) Triller said: The expansion of women's rights is the highest principle of all social evolution. A woman's heart is the source of her soul and wisdom!

(4) Napoleon, the first Emperor of France, said: Without women in the palace, it is like a year without spring, and even more like spring without beautiful roses!

(5) Bocknick, a senior official of the German drinking group, said: Our women maintain the highest value and the most important power in their bodies!

After reading it, I feel that the position of women in the national products world is also so important! Without women promoting, wholeheartedly loving the country and purchasing national products, the national products world is really terrible! Women can be said to be the hub of the rise and fall of national products! The authority in the national products world! Don't just exist in form but be dead in heart! I hope you will bring out the power of your mothers and daughters to do something earnestly, to achieve some results, and to show some color to everyone. Don't live in contradictions every day and lose the position of women! Tian Renzheng, who "sells national products well," is seeking your help to achieve success!

National Products Entertainment

New Opening Chapter for Persuading Compatriots to Use National Products (1) 236

— Zhang Mengfei

Now society loves being modern, extremely desirous of extravagance beyond description. The prosperity of Shanghai is called sleepless, and modern women are up-to-date. Snow flower powder and perfume essence come from Paris, the capital of France. White-bearded watches show the time, transported from Switzerland with a famous reputation. The clothes on the body are imported goods, and the leather shoes make a rustling sound with high heels. Diamonds turn their heads and shine their eyes. Calculated, a whole body is worth thousands of gold. The furniture at home is from Western Europe and North America, and all kinds of utensils are from foreign countries. This causes domestic money to flow outward. It is difficult to calculate the leaking cup, and it is really heartbreaking. She also says that imported goods are the most modern, but she knows that they have misunderstood the meaning of modern. Why must modern be foreign people? Chinese national products are also modern. Look at the gorgeous silk and satin, and the gauze and cotton cloth are rarely compared, far better than wool by thousands of points. Other goods are not much worse. Why send money to foreigners? Chinese goods are of good quality and low price, and can be said to be satisfactory everywhere. Since national products have been promoted, it is both patriotic and modern. It is known that modern was originally interpreted as contradictory. Sure enough, contradictions are not clear. This year's National Products Year is about to pass, but national products must still be kept in mind. Everyone promotes Chinese goods, and I advise the female compatriots, as the ancients said, that united will is an impregnable stronghold.

Family Visit Record

Madam Pan Gongzhan By Yu Qiacheng 237

—

"The market for foreign goods is almost entirely dominated by urban women, especially those urban women who are knowledgeable or

modernized. Therefore, the people who should be advocated in the Women's National Products Year, rather than rural women or uneducated women, are more accurately those urban women who are knowledgeable." Madam Tang Guanyu, the wife of Pan Gongzhan, spoke very sadly and practically at the opening ceremony of the Women's National Products Year.

At the beginning of the cold winter, sparse snowflakes fluttered around the house, and I went to visit Madam Pan.

The guest room was quiet, without any extraneous sounds. The arrangement was not very luxurious, and the tables and chairs were distributed in an orderly manner; especially the chimes coming from the adjacent study contained poetic meaning. Although this place is in the city, there is no urban noise.

Madam Pan, who is about thirty years old, wearing a national product silk dress, walked down from the upstairs.

I came specifically to solicit opinions on the work of the Women's National Products Year. After I raised this question, she pondered for a while and replied:

"This year, various groups have designated it as the Women's National Products Year, which means that women should promote national products and revitalize industries. Originally, last year was National Products Year, and adding the word 'women' this year is nothing more than wanting women to do more. However, I think that the work of this year's Women's National Products movement requires everyone to unite, and everyone to jointly take responsibility, to recover rights and interests for the country and nation in this period of national crisis filled with wind and rain"!

Then, Madam Pan also put forward her own opinions, hoping that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other industrial and commercial groups would carefully conduct an investigation, not only for inferior goods and hateful goods, but also for general imported goods, so that they are separated from our national products; because the responsibility of the women's world is to promote, and establishing a standard is the help that industrial groups should provide.

Perhaps some people do not understand why women should specifically be responsible for promoting national products? Madam Pan has a strong reason here:

"We women promote national products, and we must have this view, that is, not to let our precious children become slaves to a perished country in the future!"

There is no mother in the world who does not love her children. If we extend our maternal love to protect national products, for the sake of our children, it is always worthwhile for our women to work hard to promote national products. Does that mean that men have no responsibility in Women's National Products Year? On the passive side, they should also provide some help.

"At the same time, I hope that men will not envy the need for modernity, so that their wives can go from frugality to promoting national products!" When Madam Pan's conversation turned to this point, she expressed the hopes of the general women on their behalf.

After that, we also talked about family affairs and children's issues. From Madam Pan's opinions, I recognized that she was always thinking about the future of the young children, so all the methods can be generally said to be child-centered. Originally, in this era, so-called modern ladies have no reason to abandon the normal life of the family (neither participating in labor for economic reasons, nor participating in social undertakings for political reasons). If we return to the child-centered view, not only can we reduce some of the current bad consumption, but also contribute to the future of our nation, which is so great!

In order to study the methods of raising children, we also talked about the social status of Chinese women. She felt that the usual unnecessary caution of general mothers was the result of society's restraint on women. However, she is still very optimistic, believing that in the past, Chinese women have had famous female writers, as well as female heroes who joined the army and fought, and also women who obtained political power, so her conclusion is:

"What history tells us shows that women are not weak!"

After the conversation, I said goodbye and went out. Before parting, Madam Pan repeatedly urged me about the work of this year's Women's National Products Year:

"The most important thing is the investigation work."

Free Talk

Bondage 238

— Yu

In ancient times, people conquered animals, reducing jackals to house dogs, and domesticating wild cattle and sheep into tame cattle and sheep. Later generations used the same method to conquer mankind, tightly wrapping the feet of women, and piercing their ears with needles, and binding their chests with belts. For men, there were many decorations and restraints——anciently called etiquette——bowing and making obeisance, and the clanging of jade pendants, to make people unable to jump, unable to run, and even more unable to somersault.

What is not the same in literature! Seven-character quatrains and five-character ancient poems, level and oblique tones, are nothing more than to obliterate poetic sentiment and completely restrain nature, and then twist and pinch in dozens of words, claiming to have skill. In writing, I learn Yan, and you learn Liu. For example, after the Jiaqing Emperor changed a few words in the memorials, he made the writing of an era tend to be vulgar, and no one dared to write an ancient word or use a rare word. Later, even someone as enlightened as Zhang Wenxiang still babbled a lot when testing scholars in Sichuan, telling the scholars how to write the words and how to omit strokes. However, almost everyone who writes or composes boasts: At least mine is better than yours!

However, the modern era is the twentieth century! People all say that. But although the West is a century after the nineteenth century and before the twenty-first century, it does not seem appropriate to call it that in China. We should call ourselves the two thousand four hundred and something years after the birth of Confucius. We simply cannot get rid of the old bondage, let alone a new enlightenment. As soon as we reform, we immediately return to the old ways. It is always the desolation of autumn, without the development of spring. We abandon regulated verse to write sonnets, discard the Four Books and taste root records to pick up literary guides, abandon turbans and add square doctoral hats, and pick up fountain pens to write "Kneeling report Fu An." Why is that?

The masses are now striving to drill into the old nets, binding themselves, thinking that they are blessed and very civilized! On the contrary, they ridicule and persecute free souls, wanting to drag them down to destruction. But as the old saying goes, "Stones pressing grass never kills," free life cannot be suppressed!

Talking about the Japanese By Mu Mutian 239

—

Anyone who has not been to Japan proper, I am afraid that no one will believe that there are good people in Japan. Seeing the Japanese ronin who create bandits in "Manchuria", seeing the Japanese ronin who sell opium and traffic in handguns in "Manchuria", seeing the Japanese prostitutes who run brothels, we may arbitrarily say that they represent the entirety of the Japanese people, that they represent the "Yamato race."

Indeed, the Japanese residents in "Manchuria" have never given me a good impression. I always thought they were the embodiment of "evil." When I was young, I always thought that the Japanese were all like that. My concept of the Japanese, I am afraid, would never have changed if I had not lived in Japan proper.

However, things cannot be generalized from one aspect. No matter which country it is, there are good people and bad people. When I went to Japan to study, my concept of the Japanese changed. When I first arrived in Japan, I directly felt that the Japanese in their own country treated the Chinese much better than those "residents" in "Manchuria." At least, there was no such fierce look as in "Manchuria." Later, after entering school and the language became fluent, I met some Japanese friends who I could talk to. At that time, I felt that there were also good people among the Japanese.

The few years of living in the outer prefectures made me feel even more amiable towards the Japanese. I found the Japanese to be simple and naive. Although I was a foreigner, a "Chinese" who they despised, some Japanese people seemed not to discriminate against me. Naturally, the Japanese people I met were neither warlords, nor chaebols, nor policemen, but simple people who ran small shops, farmed the land, sold flowers, and so on. I felt that I was living comfortably and leisurely, and I was not placed in an atmosphere of oppression.

In the summer of 1924, Mr. □ and I went to the Ito coast and lived in a farmer's home. There, I really felt incredible. In that farmer's home, there was an old woman in her fifties who still went to work in the fields on the mountains in the hot weather of August. She did not know the world situation, let alone the Sino-Japanese relationship. She talked to us about everything, when the sea breeze blew at night, and we sat on the stones by the roadside and talked. The naive and kind appearance was something I had never seen before. It is said that there are many such simple-minded people in Japanese rural areas.

However, this does not mean that there are no bad people in Japan proper. Bad people naturally exist everywhere. In Ito Temple, I met a monk who owned huge temple property, and every year, he still "transformed" a lot of alms money. He ate very well, and had a wife and three sons. (It is common for monks to marry wives in Japan.) However, from his words, we discovered that he had a lot of conspiracies. And some of the teachers in the school also looked down on us.

Another time, coming back from Tokyo, I met a Japanese man on the train who said that he had come to "Manchuria" to make a living, and very politely asked us to take care of him along the way. Although not a simple person, he was not like a ronin. He behaved well all the way. However, on the Korean railway, after contacting several other Japanese people on the same train, he changed a little. After arriving in Andong, perhaps because he heard the conversations of other "residents" and understood his own position, he solemnly put on the air of a citizen of the first-class country. He did not even speak to us.

In short, if we have the opportunity to have further contact with the Japanese, we can know that among them, there are bad and good.

X X X

The room was crowded with people——father, mother, uncle, aunt, several children——everyone was silent.

The aunt lightly walked in and out, bringing tea and water…

Standing opposite the father was a doctor, wiping the gauze with a medicinal needle, slightly shaking his head, and forcefully blowing out the kerosene lamp.

Death 240

— Shi Meng

"Give her a shot of a heart stimulant, see if that helps," the doctor said softly, drawing some liquid from a vial.

………………

Grandmother lay on the bed, her face changing from pale to ashen. Her eyes were slightly open, as if covered by a white film, with no light in them. Her mouth was also open, and she was breathing with difficulty, her chest rising and falling violently.

The doctor took the needle and approached the bed:

"Lift her up a bit, so I can give her the shot."

Aunt put her hand behind Grandmother's back, preparing to lift her up, but immediately withdrew her hand.

"Doctor, just give it like that! I can't lift her, her back is stiff..." Aunt's eyes were filled with tears.

"Don't give the shot, I..."

The slurred voice broke off, the trembling mouth seemed to still be speaking, finally nodding, as if saying "Goodbye," and her eyes gradually closed.

"Give her the shot!" Aunt shouted, "Give her a heart stimulant!" Tears welled up in her eyes.

"Can't give it anymore."

"Give it! I want to see my mother for a little longer!"

Grandmother seemed about to cough up phlegm, but the phlegm got stuck in her throat, blocking her breathing, and the movement in her chest ceased.

Aunt jumped to the bedside, threw herself on Grandmother, crying and shouting like mad, touching Grandmother's face:

"She's not dead yet! She's not dead yet! Her nose is still warm! Give her the shot..."

But soon, the room was filled with weeping.

Folk Song - Ode to a Stepmother 241

— Zhen

The crow caws, "Caw, caw,"

If you have money, don't marry a stepmother.

Stepmothers have no heart,

Good clothes, they don't let me wear,

Good food, they don't let me taste.

Beaten three times a day,

Beaten nine times in three days;

Before the tears are dry,

They want me to call her "Dear Mother."

Returning Home (Continued) 242

— Wei Jinzhi

"What are you saying?" She was almost angry, her face flushed red, her strong personality revealed without concealment. "I'm telling you!" She said seriously, "I came out to work outside to make a living, to live independently. Last year, I earned some money, but not much, and I didn't want to go back like that, so I didn't. But this year, someone came to tell me: Last Chinese New Year, there were only my parents, my second brother, and my little niece at home. As soon as New Year's came, my second brother went to gamble in the village; my mother went to the temple to chant New Year's prayers; and a niece, wouldn't she go play with the other children during the New Year? So, the house was empty, with only my father. It was New Year's, and even the first day of the New Year! A family can't just close their doors, or would it still be a family? But our house has two doors, a front door and a back door, and there was only my father. So he walked from the front door to the back door, and from the back door to the front door, and there were so many people coming and going for the New Year. So he had no choice, even though it was the New Year, but to sit on the bed and cry!"

As she spoke, her eyes reddened, and mine warmed up as well.

Usually, I naturally thought about the state of rural economic bankruptcy, but because it was my own family's business, I had never seemed to think about it that way. Thinking about it, yes, my family was a complete example. As for me, it was because I had read a few books that I had been away for many years, and my younger sister and sister-in-law had also gone their separate ways for the sake of their future lives. Of a family of seven, half were drifting outside. A home that was usually quite lively had become deserted, scattered, and without any semblance of a family. Immediately, a picture floated in my sorrowful mind:

"The women are in the main room, eating peanuts and melon seeds, the children are rolling copper coins, all wearing new clothes, not working, gathered together, saying some unimportant things. And my father, he is sitting in a passageway connecting the main room to the side room. That place is usually his room, as if he were a spider occupying the center of my family. Now, he is also wearing the cotton robe he wore when he got married, a pair of cloth socks, a pair of shoes, sitting on the dim bed where he usually stays, not using a handkerchief or his sleeves, but wiping away tears with his own stiff and trembling hands. Those hands, they are the hands that worked hard, labored, and raised us, they should have been idle long ago, and now they are wiping away tears."

So for the second time, my eyes became hot again, I wiped away the tears, but forced a smile and said to my sister, "I'm going back, I was just teasing you, I want to go back with you."

The next day, we braved the snow and wind and returned home together!

Impressions of Hong Kong 244

— Wen Juan

The boundless blue sea, I don't know when, had one corner painted with a gray-yellow color, so these two absolutely irreconcilable colors of seawater were eternally arguing beside an isolated island, as if seeking a judgment. But this small island itself seemed to have hidden worries, just silently watching these seas and never being able to give them an answer. This small island is the famous Hong Kong, and it is also the destination of my trip this time.

When I first landed, I saw that the stores were not very grand or luxurious, and the market was very desolate. I thought to myself: Everyone says Hong Kong is good, but where exactly is Hong Kong's goodness?

I rushed to ×× Street and found □□ Jun. He has lived here for a long time and is very familiar with everything here. I told him my questions, and he just smiled without answering. After eating, he took me out for a walk. The flat, smooth roads, shaded by trees, were similar to Shanghai. But as we walked, the road under our feet gradually rose, winding around several turns, and when I looked back, I was already halfway up the mountain. Before me were crisscrossing asphalt roads, matched with the lush green hills, like countless silver-gray ribbons, tightly tied around a pile of emerald jade. The cut faces of the hills were decorated with patterns of deep yellow or brown gravel, and the crevices in the stones were filled with many unknown wildflowers. The petals were huge, and the colors were bright, probably all subtropical plants. A stream flowed below the mountain path, though artificially constructed, the sound of its murmuring was very pleasant. Black iron railings wound around all the mountain roads and both sides of the ditches, looking like a spider web from a distance. A car suddenly emerged from the flower and tree woven screen and disappeared into the depths of the jungle. Countless buildings of different colors hid under the green shade, quietly dreaming their beautiful dreams. There was no sound around, only the barking of mountain dogs broke the silence of the space.

"It's an absolutely beautiful big garden!" I exclaimed at the panorama of Hong Kong.

"A desolate island in the hands of the Chinese, once it falls into the hands of the British, becomes a scenic spot. From the national point of view, ceding land is certainly an unfortunate thing, but for the Chinese living here, especially the Chinese who love order and are rich in aesthetic appreciation, perhaps there is the opposite view!" As we spoke, we suddenly heard a commotion on the mountain, followed by many people running down the mountain, running and bumping into each other, shouting and laughing. The kind of disorder and disorganization, compared with the neat buildings around them, gave people an indescribable feeling. They were probably all natives of Hong Kong. The young women wore big pants (no skirts), with a large braid hanging behind their heads. Some wore silver bracelets on their hands, while others did not wear bracelets but wore anklets. The older ones mostly wore buns, with hairpins and earrings, similar to the dress of the Yangtze River area twenty years ago. The men who accompanied them had no braids and held birdcages and pipes in their hands. Judging from the appearance of their skin, nutrition, and gorgeous clothing, they had a good material life, but in their expressions and words, it was impossible to find a trace of education. These are probably the typical good people in the colony.

When going down the mountain, the fragrance of flowers, the gentleness and breath of the sea, and the strong smell of opium smoke mixed together. Their eternally irreconcilable breath may be the characteristic of Hong Kong.

Last Letter (7) 245

— Lin Huiyin

"Then, when are you going to tell them? How about I go with you now?"

"Go? I have some other things to do. I have to go to the office later. I'll give you an answer within a day or two."

A day passed, no answer; two days passed, no answer. It was Saturday, the 27th; by that afternoon, Yina couldn't bear it anymore, she could only go find Xi Zhuoyun again.

"You're here, I was just about to write you a letter," Zhuoyun said, while inviting Yina to sit down.

She sat down in the guest seat she was used to, but didn't say anything.

"Things might be a bit bad. Listen to me. Originally, the staff here could get an advance on their salary for this month, but this month is the end of the year, when everyone needs money, but the manager has issued a notice saying that no one can get an advance on their salary. We pushed two representatives to ask, but they were rejected. Think about it, they treat the staff here so harshly, let alone outsiders like you? Not to mention that your novel hasn't been signed yet, so you can't get paid, even the published ones, and even the royalties for January, have been decided not to be paid. Several people have already come to ask for royalties, but there's no way."

Yina didn't say anything, just stared at him.

He was casually flipping through the books, letters, and so on on the table. Finally, he pulled out a letter and gave it to Yina.

She thought it was about her business, but after reading it, she knew it was a proofreader there writing to Xi Zhuoyun. Because the proofreader heard that his position was in danger, he was begging Xi Zhuoyun for help. After she finished reading it, she handed the letter back to him, wondering why he wanted her to read that letter? Was he implying to her that the letter she wrote to him was not humble enough, compared to the proofreader's letter? Or was he boasting that someone was begging him? Would he see her as one of the people begging him? Would he show the letter she gave him to others, just like he just showed her the proofreader's letter? Why did he want her to read that letter?

"You see, there's no way," he said with a sigh, seeing that she didn't say anything.

Yina felt that her eyes were a little dry, and forced herself to hold back.

Zhuoyun was silent for a while, and silence tightly enveloped them.

Grains, Marked Flour Weak and Powerless 261

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the market for each month was generally flat and weak. As quotations for foreign wheat in Chicago continued to decline by about 3-4 jiao, and those in Canada declined by 1 jiao, market sentiment remained flat and weak after opening. Transactions were not numerous. All groups of actual sales customers felt that purchases were light and unanimously waited and watched. Therefore, although most manufacturers still agreed not to sell, they ultimately could not reverse the actual trend. When the market opened in the afternoon, each month generally hovered, and transactions were also exceptionally quiet. It was only heard that small factories had slightly hedged sales, so the market sentiment was slightly weak. Looking at the future situation, there is little opportunity for recovery. As a result, the current month was unchanged, April and May were down by 7.5 li, June and July were unchanged, and August was down by 2.5 li.

Wheat Futures Benefit from Rainy Weather 262

Yesterday, after the wheat futures market opened in the morning, each month was unusually quiet. Only a few cars were opened for August, and the rest were empty. When the market opened in the afternoon, transactions were relatively active. Market sentiment was slightly higher due to the rainy weather. Whether considering the facts or comparing various grain prices, it is feared that there may be changes in the market value of new wheat this year. As a result, April and July were better by 1 fen, and August was better by 3 fen. Spot wheat also showed weak signs, with prices down by 3-5 fen compared to the peak price. Bengbu wheat opened at 3 yuan 4 jiao 7 fen, Yaowan wheat at 3 yuan 5 jiao 7 fen, Yingzhou wheat at 3 yuan 4 jiao 8 fen, and Nansuzhou wheat at 3 yuan 3 jiao 6 fen, totaling 3,200 bags, reportedly purchased by Fuxin.

Rice Market, Ship's Foot Stalled by Rain 263

Yesterday, the sources in South Shanghai were 40-50 boats (over 6,000 shih), but due to continuous rainy weather, very few customers came to the market, and transactions were scarce. The situation was even quieter. The ship's foot was stalled by the rain, and the situation was virtually stagnant. As sources were plentiful, the market inevitably slumped. For example, the prices of regular bang su, tong, nan, gang, etc. purchased by this street were all reduced by 5 fen, and although the appetite of customer bang was somewhat active, the number was limited. The northern bang purchased a total of over 1,000 bags, and the southern bang did not take any. Although sellers repeatedly tried to tighten the market for late rice, the soft prices of Qingjiao, Sijing, and Xilian, etc. were down by 3-4 fen due to flat customer intentions. Duyangjian's sales were better and could still stand firm. The color of the Metamorphosis Yin Yuan was slightly softer, and the price remained largely unchanged.

Ningbo and Oujiang Actively Purchase Customer Rice 264

Yesterday, the market for customer rice continued to arrive, but sales were very active. This street and the Fujian bang are still watching, but the Wenzhou bang from Zhejiang Province continues to purchase smoothly, with a strong appetite. The Ningdu bang is also making inquiries. Market sentiment and the market have gradually become firmer. The prices of high-grade goods in each stall have uniformly increased by 3-5 fen, while medium and low-grade goods remain flat. The entire city purchased 405 bags of coarse rice from Shashi, 1,230 bags of sen rice from Nanjing and Wuhu, and 180 bags of Jingliu coarse rice from Ningbo, with no other transactions. The market shape remains firm.

Soybean Factories Purchase Well 265

Yesterday, the soybean market temporarily stabilized. Factories had a good appetite for purchases. Xiamen, Fuzhou, Ningbo, this street, and inland areas all actively purchased, so the market sentiment was slightly flat. Yesterday, factories reportedly purchased 11-12 cars of Yingzhou beans, priced from 2 yuan 4 jiao 8 fen to 4 jiao 5 fen, and 4 cars of Nanhe beans, priced at 2 yuan 4 jiao 5 fen. Two cars of Bozhou beans were also transacted, priced at 2 yuan 4 jiao 2 fen. There were also 4-5 cars of Guide beans, and although they were not transacted, the difference between the buying and selling price was only 1-2 fen, so a transaction may be possible. Other gangs also transacted 6-7 cars of various beans.

Sugar Market, Chaozhou Raw Sugar Continues to Open 266

Yesterday, the sugar market saw little trading because the customs was closing today. The association's pricing for No. 24 coarse granulated white was 19 yuan 9 jiao, but no transactions were made. Over a hundred bags of domestic Chaozhou raw sugar were opened, priced from 11 yuan 8 jiao 5 fen, 7 jiao 5 fen, to 5 jiao. No. 1 Mianbai from this factory was priced at 18 yuan 4 jiao 5 fen and 18 yuan 3 jiao 5 fen, with some sporadic transactions. Hainan red sugar continues to arrive, priced at 13 yuan 4-5 jiao for the upper grades and around 13 yuan for the lower grades. Yesterday, the Qingyuan ship transported 357 bags of green sugar and 21 bags of Zhiyang. The Yisheng ship transported 173 bags of Zhiyang, 69 bags of green sugar, and 31 bags of red sand. In addition, there were a total of 269 bags of transit goods.

Dried Goods, Chaozhou Fermented Rice Sells Well, Market Sentiment is Firm 267

Since the red rice from Shantou opened at a red price, the market has been stagnant for a long time due to sluggish customer sales. Recently, the northern gang has started to purchase, and the Tianjin gang is also actively inquiring, so the market has turned bullish. High-grade Zhuang needs 35 yuan, and secondary goods range from 30 yuan to 28 yuan. Ordinary goods are 20 yuan. It is heard that there is not much inventory left, and arrivals are not strong, so the market is expected to tighten.

Orchid Seeds, High-Grade Goods Extremely Scarce 268

Medium-grade products from Zhangzhou orchid are extremely scarce. For example, goods that are completely yellow have opened at 48 yuan. However, the 20 pieces that arrived earlier did not open due to their poor color. Yesterday, it was heard that the Taiyuan ship loaded 21 pieces, and samples are expected to be seen today. If the color is bright yellow, clean, and free of sand, the previous price can still be maintained.

Silk and Tea, Overseas Chinese Silk No One Inquires 269

[Guangdong Factory Silk Shipped to Shanghai for Sale] Due to the rampant decline and encroachment on sales by Japanese silk in overseas markets, the market price of white factory silk in Guangdong has plummeted, and there are still few inquiries. The spring cocoons in Guangdong province will soon be on the market, and the silk is still thick. They are shipped to Shanghai for sale. Recently, domestic silk weavers, seeing that the opening price of Guangdong silk is less than 400 yuan per package (80 catties) and the quality is excellent, are rushing to buy it. As a result, the sales of Jiangzhe white factories through the silk door are increasingly deteriorating.

[Dou Gong Silk Supply Cannot Meet Demand] The only Dou Gong silk factory in this port is Fulunheng, which is working as usual. Silk production is limited, and demand in India is still strong, so supply cannot meet demand. This ten-day period only saw 34 packages of Dou Gong silk shipped to India and Switzerland.

[White Factory Jing Has Price but No Market] Silk prices in European and American markets are still falling, and no one is inquiring about Chinese silk. There is still a lot of silk in Shanghai. In the blink of an eye, new cocoons will be on the market. Although Chinese silk merchants are eager to sell, the losses are huge. Each package of Shanghai white factory Jing needs to lose more than 200 yuan, but there is still a price but no market. There is no way to dump it, and the market is in a slump. Yesterday, only Indian Zhuang entered 7 packages of yellow coarse silk and 10 packages of white tu silk, and prices were all trending downwards.

Piece Goods, Rubber-Coated Cloth Sales Smooth, Prices Buoyant 270

There are two types of raincoat cloth, thick and thin, with many patterns and names. Recently, thin goods like elephant skin lining cloth have been selling poorly. The only type that is active and selling well in the market is single-sided rubber-coated cloth. 70-80% of the wool and clothing stores on this street are selling it. Although thin goods are cheap, there is no demand. This spring, single-sided rubber-coated raincoat cloth sold for a high of 5 yuan 5 jiao and a low of 5 yuan 1 jiao 5 fen. Currently, the standard market price is a good 5 yuan 3 jiao, because sales have been smooth due to the continuous rainy weather.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Not Optimistic 291

– Qiong Sheng

Recently, Mr. Tang Youren, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, who returned from inspecting diplomacy in North China, gave a speech on the 24th regarding his observations over the past year. He stated: "Wherever I went, I was filled with many emotions that cannot be fully expressed in a single sentence." However, in short, the situation in North China is "not optimistic. How it will evolve depends on how we make continuous efforts in internal affairs and diplomacy."

After carefully listening to this restrained yet meaningful speech, we sigh and lament at its implications, and also feel a sense of warning and encouragement. Since the "September 18th Incident," when the cannons roared, the northeastern provinces were lost in an instant. Our already weakened China has contracted a serious illness due to an acute cold. Just as a dying person prays for God's forgiveness, many people are celebrating that the League of Nations, the "God of Peace," adopted the Lytton Report and passed a resolution not recognizing the puppet organization, believing that "justice has been served" and that diplomacy has triumphed. However, our clog-wearing friends, who are determined to implement their continental policy, will not be deterred by a unanimous League of Nations resolution except for the removal of dissenting votes. Moreover, understanding the principle that strength can overcome softness, they will certainly not be satisfied with merely three provinces. Therefore, once Shanhaiguan was lost, Rehe immediately changed color, and the situation in eastern Luan became urgent. We had no choice but to embrace the principle of "peace," to understand each other, and to seek tranquility by appeasement.

However, the ceasefire agreement demarcated by a demilitarized zone is as ridiculous as demarcating a border with a Hong ditch. Not only can our clog-wearing friends use pretexts to invade at any time, but just as Emperor Gaozu of Han deployed troops at Guangwu to closely monitor Pengcheng, the war zone has become a means of political and economic control over North China. Therefore, although the evil specter of war has vanished with the gentle breeze of peace, another rising political and economic force has suppressed North China. Remotely, recovering Shanhaiguan and the passes of the Great Wall is more difficult than conquering Jingzhou. Not only has it not been completed in a year, but it is no longer in its original state. More recently, the military exercises in Peiping and Tianjin are nothing less than a strong military presence threatening the border.

These are the obvious things. As for other trivial matters, how can we not find a trace of them? When the puppet officials took the stage, the Japanese concession in Tianjin widely publicized and celebrated; Yoshiko Kawashima, a well-known and typical devil who had performed extraordinary feats in the Northeast and Shanghai, toured Beiping; and Tadashi Araki secretly visited foreign churches to investigate their addresses and properties. These events echoed the issues of Inner Mongolia and Xinjiang independence. As for the fact that "inferior goods" are flooding the provinces of North China, even causing the Jiaoji Railway to become "prosperous," we look to the future but do not want to speak of it, nor can we bear to speak of it, for we are also "filled with many emotions that cannot be fully expressed in a single sentence."

The ancients said: "Trust is the foundation of a nation. Only with prestige can one gain trust." Under such circumstances of the guest dominating the host, the situation in North China is probably truly, as Mr. Tang said, "not optimistic." What shall we do?

Wife and Lover 292

– Skinny

Wife is an ominous word. Those who have wives generally do not love their wives, but only their lovers. Lovers are truly sweet things. No matter how good a wife is, she is still ordinary because you have "played" with her for too long. Therefore, you do not appreciate her goodness. A lover, on the other hand, is someone you can approach but not get too close to, and the relationship is often semi-public. You cannot fully enjoy the pleasure, so you feel that the aftertaste is incomplete and especially worth cherishing. Therefore, the ancients said it well: "A wife is not as good as a concubine, a concubine is not as good as a maid, a maid is not as good as something stolen, and something stolen is not as good as something you cannot steal." This truly explains the secret of wives and lovers. People just like to do things secretly. The more secretive it is, the more novel it feels. Once it becomes public, it becomes bland. Desire is a strange thing.

Why do people only love lovers and not wives? Ordinary people think that this is due to the human nature of "loving the new and disliking the old." But that is not the case. It is entirely determined by objective society and material relations. When human society first began, the union of the two sexes was originally natural and instinctive. Later, due to the emergence of property relations, and unfortunately these property relations were seized by men, women became appendages of men, and then playthings. After years of ritual and education, women became a slave class forever under the rule of men. Now, as the essence of society changes from a feudal economy to a capitalist economy, the status of women also changes. It transforms from a feudal nature to a capitalist nature, which means that women were previously regulated by rituals and education, but now they are regulated by money. In the past, women were victims of feudal rituals and education; now, they are victims of the money of capitalists. In the past, women succumbed to rituals and education; now, women succumb to money. In the past, women were prisoners of rituals and education; now, women are prisoners of money. Women have transformed from chaste women and virtuous women under the feudal rituals and education to commodities in the market of capitalist society that can be bought and sold by anyone with money. This is the current situation. From the above, we can see that women have become appendages of men from the beginning due to social material relations. The reason why women have become playthings, allowing men to display their instinct to dislike the old and love the new at any time, and why women cannot independently advocate their union with the opposite sex, is because these social material relations have destroyed the natural union of the two sexes based on human instinct, creating this unequal phenomenon between men and women. We can understand this clearly from the above explanation.

Because the union of the two sexes is now not due to instinctive natural requirements but due to material relations, there is no so-called loving union between the two sexes except for naked vested interests. No matter how thick you say love is, in the final analysis, it is just a combination of vested interests. However, this fundamental vested interest is often concealed by the passionate desire on the surface. The beautiful women embraced by the young masters can also be said to be a union of love on the surface, but in fact, who dares to say that they were not bought with money? If they were not bought with money, then why do the beautiful women in the world belong exclusively to the rich, while poor scholars can only find some unremarkable ordinary women? Since the current union of the two sexes is entirely based on naked vested interests rather than on instinctive natural union, its foundation is understandably unstable. Since a man can buy this woman with money, he can certainly buy another woman with money. On the woman's side, since she can sell herself to this man because of vested interests, she can certainly sell herself to someone else when these vested interests change, that is, when this man cannot satisfy the woman's desires. In this way, marriage becomes a sin, love becomes shaken, and everyone sighs that marriage and love have completely gone bankrupt.

Has marriage and love really gone bankrupt? "Marriage is the tomb of love." Is marriage really the tomb of love? Of course not! As long as the material relations of this society change, all problems can be solved.

Is Marriage the Tomb of Love? 294

— Xinzi

(Part 1)

The question of whether marriage is the tomb of love has only become apparent and loudly proclaimed in modern times. Especially after the evil arrows of capitalism have spread throughout the world, many bizarre and complex phenomena that people cannot clearly explain have occurred. There is no way to correctly resolve the entangled major issue of marriage and love, so people passively shout: Marriage is the tomb of love. Recently, New Shanghai published Ms. Ruizhu's "Marriage is Not the Tomb of Love," which is exactly the opposite of her argument. Her argument is almost derived from the empty conclusion she reached through the analysis and proof of her so-called personal experience of marriage. Moreover, she concludes forcefully: "In short, if young men and women can love each other with sincerity and unconditionally, then who says that getting married will not make you feel the pain of love entering the tomb?"

The theories of both sides are one-sided, failing to fully expand, and only superficially describing the external aspect of the phenomenon. They both inherit the ancestral logical method, observing the ever-changing social phenomena of capitalist society with an isolated and static perspective, lightly regarding a corner of social phenomena as objective and true existence.

Originally, both marriage and love are a necessary and reasonable matter that the human race properly needs both physiologically and mentally. It has no sin in itself. That is, both marriage and love are basic things necessary for the social life of the human race. So why do reasonable things cause many tragedies and become as terrible as entering a tomb in people's eyes? This is entirely the fault given to it by the bad economic foundation of society! Let's turn over the history of the development of married life and we can understand that marriage has not been sending love to the grave from the beginning. It was not until a certain stage of social life changed, giving marriage pain, causing many tragedies or after marriage, which strongly affect love. Therefore, in the feudal society, people dared not file for divorce due to the authority of the old etiquette. When it came to capitalist society, people could freely combine and separate, so the question was loudly raised, thinking that love is sacred and joyful, and marriage is annoying and painful. Indeed, under such an unreasonable social system, people's married life has therefore produced many unreasonable phenomena, but these are all reflections of the miserable social life given to them!

Visiting the Sick 296

— Yuan

When I was about to attend the second class in the morning, I received a letter from Man. Seeing his large handwriting, my hands were already shaking. What's more, the letter really reported bad news to me: he was sick. My heart was beating, and my whole body felt a little cold as if the blood was contracting. I didn't know what to do!

That class was with Huan Qin. I didn't have time to ask for leave, so I asked Xiao Chen and Mr. × to explain, and immediately ran out of the school gate. Usually there are so many rickshaws, but today there were none. It seemed like they were deliberately making things difficult for me and hiding. The section of road from the Chinese area to the concession didn't feel annoying usually, but today when people have something on their minds and want to walk fast, the stones and mud on the road are hindering your movement, which is really killing me. After running across the bridge, I was covered in sweat. It took me a long time to see a rickshaw. I didn't bother to bargain with him, sat down and told him to run fast. He was really running with all his might, but the speed of my hope was always much faster than his running. Compared to him, my heart seemed to be running like a car, while his legs were walking like an ox cart, which really made me angry. I kept telling him to hurry up, and thinking about it calmly, I also found it funny. Usually when I sit in a rickshaw, I like to see the trees by the roadside, paying attention to whether they are sprouting and growing leaves, or looking at the men and women walking on the road, commenting on this and that. Today, I can't see anything in my eyes, and I imagine Man's sick appearance in front of me, and I'm anxious to know what disease he has. The last time I saw him a few days ago, wasn't he still fine? How could he have gotten sick? I suddenly remembered reading in the newspaper that the weather has been unstable since spring, and there are many patients, especially children with smallpox, and there are even more people with colds everywhere. Does he have a cold? Does he have smallpox? No, smallpox is a children's disease, how could he have smallpox!

After getting out of the car, I hurriedly knocked on his door, entered the door, went upstairs, and when I entered his room, I saw that he had put down the burden he was carrying, and relaxed.

He only had a minor illness, so I was relieved.

On the Future of Movie Stars 297

— Jun

Due to the economic downturn, all businesses have been severely hit, and people of all salary classes are particularly terrified. Unfortunate encounters such as salary reductions and layoffs are recorded in the news almost every day. Not to mention other things, just looking at the insecure state of life of practitioners in the film industry is enough to make people sigh.

Because they feel that the future is bleak and the current supply cannot be met, everyone has planted the desire to change careers. The brave ones go to implement it, and there are certainly not a few who are hesitant, but everyone has this kind of psychology to some extent. And becoming a dancer has become an outlet for ordinary female movie stars when there is no way out. Their reasoning is: the income of dancers is much stronger than that of movie actors. In order to obtain a comfortable material environment, they would rather do that kind of life being embraced than continue to work hard as a movie actor, which is of course much more enjoyable. This fact has been proven by Liang Saizhen before, and yesterday a newspaper also reported that Xuan Jinglin is also going to be a dancer. Although there are not many initiators yet, it is difficult to predict who will follow in the future. Originally, changing from a movie star to a dancer is just a personal career change, which is not worth making a fuss about. However, under this kind of continuous occurrence, we cannot completely ignore it. Is it only when movie stars have no other choice that they become dancers, or have they already recognized that dancers are the only way out? If they are only for their own material life and abandon their work and tasks to accommodate a luxurious life that only cares about the present, then there is no meaning to speak of, and it is not desirable for wise people. The film career is certainly difficult, but it does not seem to be in a situation where there is no way to maintain it, and the future of the film is not without the possibility of development. If you work hard a little bit, you may gain more in the future. In terms of social views, it is always more meaningful than being a dancer.

In short, if you simply become a dancer because you are dazzled by the temptation of material desires, no matter how sufficient the reason is, it cannot be regarded as a correct behavior. As for those who intend to use the trademark of a star to promote their business, it not only insults the star's own reputation, but also is a scum in the film industry. All those who are truly engaged in the film industry should pay serious attention to prevent the occurrence of similar events, so that the film front will not form a collapse, and save the film industry in case of emergency.

A Rainy Spring Night 298

— Ren

It's raining again. The water droplets on the roof tiles are dripping on the steps, and the gusts of wind are also embellishing this quiet space. The glass is shaking against each other, suffering the impact of the wind. There is a deathly silence on the earth except for the dripping rain on the steps and the ticking clock in front of the window. Ah! Rainy night, rainy spring night!

It's midnight already, and the one who is patiently waiting has not returned yet. Maybe she will only be able to return at dawn tonight... She is already intoxicated in the arms of another man. But I dare not think like this, it's too terrible.

Another gust of wind and rain passed, hitting the doors and windows, making them rattle.

A worried person is ultimately a worried person. My whole head is burning, and I can't sleep no matter how I toss and turn. Terrible images are reflected in front of my eyes: the jazz music is anesthetizing the youth, she must be throwing herself into the arms of a gentleman, his hands are tightly hugging her, and his mouth chewing betel nut is sweetly kissing her...

It was also in such a rainy spring that I met her in her hometown. At that time, she was still a shy country girl. When she saw me, a young man returning from the metropolis, she couldn't help but fall in love with me. We once loved each other, and now we have become a nominal couple with different dreams in the same bed. We returned to Shanghai, and she was infected by the city and became who she is now.

In spirit, she is no longer my person. Yes! Nothing is better than the temptation of material things! Ah, the edification of urbanization, the powerful temptation of matter, has turned a country girl into a modern lady.

In the sleepless night, in the pouring spring rain, I curse the sins of this metropolis, and I keep shedding sad tears...

There are so many temptations in the big metropolis!

I want it, I want to take it all back.

The temptations in the big metropolis! You are the greatest enemy of young people!

Tomb Sweeping 300

— Yafei

In order to commemorate my deceased father and grandmother, I always return to my hometown once a year to sweep the tomb as usual. This is considered fulfilling the duty of a son!

Although it is already spring these days, there is no warmth at all, and it is still very cold. Moreover, the weather is so dry that the water in the river is almost drying up.

I took the 8 o'clock express train to Suzhou on March 7; in some places, because the water was too shallow, the small steamship stopped running. We specially hired a small gasoline boat. When we arrived at Xukou, the northwest wind howled again. Later, we still drove back to Muduo, preparing to open again early tomorrow morning. After dinner: after 7 o'clock, I saw that the wind seemed to be quiet. So everyone discussed taking a night boat. At this time, fortunately, the sky was full of many stars, and the light from the stars could vaguely distinguish all the scenery in nature. We arrived at our hometown at 11 o'clock, a hometown that we had been away from for a long time.

The god of night opened his huge wings, shrouding the entire earth. In the desolate mountains and fields, everything seemed silent, so silent that it was terrible!

At this time, the shops in the town were all closed. Before my eyes, there were only a few vertical and horizontal streets, lying quietly. There was no place to buy lights, so I had to grope by the light of some stars. The rugged roads and the dilapidated bridges really made me feel that it was difficult to move my feet. The cold air was unbearable for us. But, we finally found our old home, which was a dilapidated house with three rafters, guarded by an inheriting grandmother. However, although I had only not seen this grandmother for a year, she was even more old and decrepit.

The next day, the weather was so clear. We prepared sacrifices and paper money to go to the graves of our grandfather and father to pay our respects.

When I stepped on the cemetery mountain and patrolled the tombs of my grandmother and father, I thought of my father and recalled my grandmother, and I couldn't help but let two lines of tears wet my clothes. The remains of my grandmother and father seemed to be emerging in front of my eyes; but, but, how did they know that I, this unfilial grandson, was missing them here? They can't come to comfort my empty soul. They worked hard all their lives, only leaving us a few mountains, a few fields, and a few houses, but my grandmother died so young that my grandfather died, and my father left the world so young, and my mother had already been widowed for a long time. I am now also the father of a child. So, what will I leave to my child? What will I have to comfort the deceased grandmother and father, and a living mother? I can only be ashamed!

Recently, I saw myself in the mirror, and I was so old. A young man in his twenties was so old, which really shocked me!

Hot Wind (5) 301

— Cai Tonghua

"When I was sensible, a foreign dollar was worth two thousand copper coins, and one copper coin was worth two pieces of tofu, that is, meat was only a few dozen pennies; now it's the opposite, what copper plates do you want? One dollar only has two hundred and ten copper plates, and a tael of fish costs at least a few copper plates. How can you be a human being like this? I'd rather be a dog in peacetime than a citizen in troubled times. It's tiring to be a human being these days." Every time the conversation ends, it's always my mother's old saying. Although the old woman says she hates being a human being, she works hard every day, taking care of the fields and managing the household, helping her son support the lives of three people. The mother likes to tell her sons about the good things when she was young. In fact, since Ah Xing understood human affairs, didn't the family not eat a piece of white meat or a bowl of dry rice all year round except for a few major festivals? Didn't the mother also cry in distress when paying rent? Isn't she also working like a machine? Suffering from hunger, cold, and bullying? However, the mother was just energetic at that time and could handle it. What about now? Uncertainty and sadness become apparent with the mother's age and disappointment. Ah Xing was afraid to look at the mother's pensive, lifeless eyes, poured the porridge, which was almost all sweet potatoes, into his stomach, and hurriedly left.

In the east, the sun has not yet risen, only a few peach-colored clouds, the clear sky, and the mood of a girl are so quiet, and the space is filled with the refreshing breath of plants. Children sing mountain songs, leading cattle towards the small mountains to start their carefree, naughty, and romantic lives. Birds open their clear throats and sing melodiously. "Little Dogzi, you ghost." Ah Xing tore off Little Dogzi's hands, and both of them laughed. They had been used to playing together since they were young, and they were also growing their friendship from laughter, scolding, crying, and fighting; Little Dogzi took Ah Xing's shoulder, and the two of them walked happily.

"Look!" Ah Xing looked in the direction Little Dogzi was pointing, where a group of people gathered, men, women, and children, gesticulating and yelling.

"Heaven has unpredictable winds and clouds, and people have unpredictable disasters!"

"Having lived for sixty or seventy years, it's changed, the world is coming to an end!" Old man Jixiang, Uncle Shunxing's uncle, a strange old man, he didn't want to be a subject of the Qing Dynasty, or wait for the emperor to ascend the Dragon Pavilion to be sealed, but he stubbornly insisted for no apparent reason, perhaps to miss the past, he kept a silver-white braid as thick as chopsticks, coiled on his head; at this time he was also shaking his head, marveling with worldly experience.

In Uncle Shunxing's field, some of the rice that had been knocked down was draped with a gray suit and a student hat, but the hat was also gray. Apart from going to the city or when the army went to the countryside, people in the village could only see such things; these rare things brought back the sadness and terror of being pushed and donated, which was even more terrible and ominous than the division of the dead. They all kept a distance, and no one dared to touch it. Today, Aunt Shunxing, who rarely goes out, is also standing here holding her son, locking her eyebrows, reddening her eyes, and constantly looking at the sidewalk with her head stretched out, looking very anxious.
